Processes a brace pattern and returns either an expanded array (if {\ttfamily options.\+expand} is true), a highly optimized regex-\/compatible string. 

This method is called by the main \href{\#braces}{\texttt{ braces}} function.

Expands a brace pattern into an array. 

This method is called by the main \href{\#braces}{\texttt{ braces}} function when {\ttfamily options.\+expand} is true. Before using this method it\textquotesingle{}s recommended that you read the \href{\#performance}{\texttt{ performance notes}}) and advantages of using \href{\#compile}{\texttt{ .compile}} instead.

\DoxyCodeLine{console.log(\mbox{\hyperlink{es_2shared_2watch_8js_aeed07914210aa3343ae22388d40fdedb}{braces}}.expand(\textcolor{stringliteral}{'a/\{b,c\}/d'}));}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{comment}{//=> ['a/b/d', 'a/c/d'];}}
\end{DoxyCode}
